              <div class="cnCustomJsContainer" id="idCustomJsContainer">
               <script type="text/javascript">
                try
 {
     
 
   var _gaq = _gaq || [];
   _gaq.push(['_setAccount', 'UA-26480638-1']);
   _gaq.push(['_trackPageview']);
 
   (function() {
     var ga = document.createElement('script'); ga.type = 'text/javascript'; ga.async = true;
     ga.src = ('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https://ssl' : 'http://www') + '.google-analytics.com/ga.js';
     var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(ga, s);
   })();
 
 
 }
 catch(err)
 {}
               </script>
               <script type="text/javascript">
                try
 {
     
   // Scripts within this section are used to manage effects on the CVMG pages.  Initially created May 1, 2012 by Dave Dobson
 
   var elementInFocus = null;
 
   function changeDivInFocus(newDivId) {
 
     // This function assumes that another Div is already in focus and first turns it off.
 
     if (getElementInFocus() != null) {
       changeObjectStyleClass(getElementInFocus(), 'divDisplayOff');
     }
     else {
       changeObjectStyleClass(getElementByName('Page_1'),'divDisplayOff');
     }
 
     // Then it tries to find the element called 'newDivId'
     setElementInFocus(getElementByName(newDivId));
 
     // If it is found then it will be established in focus
     if (getElementInFocus() == null) {
       alert("changeDivInFocus msg - Fatal Error - Unable to find element called " , newDivId);
       return;
     }
     changeObjectStyleClass(getElementInFocus(), 'divDisplayOn');
   }
   function changeObjectStyleClass (theObject, styleClass) {
 
     // This function includes two ways to set the Style Class for the identified object.
     // This is required as Firefox and IE do not use the same reference.
 
     if (theObject == null) {
       alert("changeObjectStyleClass msg - Cannot change style class for unidentified object.");
       return;
     }
     theObject.setAttribute("class", styleClass);
     theObject.setAttribute("className", styleClass);
   }
 
   function getElementByName(elementName) {
 
     // Returns a pointer to the HTML object of the specified name.
     // Note that it is possible that no object exists in which case a Null will be returned.
 
     return document.getElementById(elementName);
   }
 
   function getElementInFocus() {
     
     // Return a pointer to previously set element in focus.
     return elementInFocus;
   }
 
   function sendMsg(msgText) {
 
     // Display an Alert message on the screen showing the text provided
     alert("sendMsg text says: '" + msgText + "'");
   }
 
   function setElementInFocus(theElement) {
 
     // Set a pointer to the element in focus
     elementInFocus = theElement;
   }
 
 
 }
 catch(err)
 {}
               </script>
